## Multilens Translation Atlas

### AQM

- `P1.1`
  Equation:

  \[\rho_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^+ = \Phi_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}}(\rho_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^-), \qquad \Phi_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} = \mathsf O_{\texttt{arody}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{kaiin}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{cheedy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{aiin}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{saraisl}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{eey}}\]

  Variable legend: `rho^-` incoming folio line state; `rho^+` outgoing line state; `Phi_line^(AQM)` source operator chain.
  Reading: essence load / salt root / cycle completion line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Game Theory

- `P1.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P1_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P1_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: essence load / salt root / cycle completion line.
  Confidence: mixed
